commit 9247c253c06ac308c9aff993609bea0e12d33803
Author: hasansayani-xilinx <44008764+hasansayani-xilinx@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Jan 29 15:30:54 2019 -0800

    2018.3 branch XMA changes 2019-01-24 (#902)
    
    * Fix log message in error path of xmares kernel reservation
    
    * Fix for kernel alloc issue via kernel affinity
    
    When a process has been allocated a kernel, attempt to locate and
    re-use that kernel instance when subsequent session requests are
    made by the same process
    
    * Changing config yaml and stats files paths
    
    * Adding exec name in xma log
    
    * Close possible race condition in init of shm db and mutex
    
    It is possible that a 2nd process mapping in the shared
    memory may do so before the mutex is initialized by the
    originating process.  This fix eliminates that possible
    error condition and introduces an up-to 500ms loop condition
    in the event that process 2 is launched before process 1
    fully initializes the shared memory region.
    
    Signed-off-by: Jeffrey Mouroux <jmouroux@xilinx.com>
    
    * Add flag to indicate resources have been programmed
    
    Signed-off-by: Jeffrey Mouroux <jmouroux@xilinx.com>
    
    * Check for existence of default directory path for cfg file
    
    Signed-off-by: Jeffrey Mouroux <jmouroux@xilinx.com>
    
    * Fixing 2018.3 XRT branch compilation issues. Seen only in 2018.3 branch and not master. Fixed #define _GNU_SOURCE and added couple of include files

commit 2433c901810d546c549729405271e0bb6dfeb367
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Wed Nov 21 11:50:13 2018 -0800

    Support CDMA base addresses per feature rom
    
    Number of changes to support CDMA as a shared resource ignored by user context.  Ultimately validation of exec buffer must ignore CUs that identify CDMA kernels.
    
    To support this, the context now tracks regular CUs separately from CDMA kernels.  The CDMA kernels, which are used as regular CUs, are added to the context when the scheduler configuration assigns them a CU idx.

Merge: 075b55a 32451fd
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>

    Lock xclbin prior to using KDS

commit 32451fd7ce19836703f42f4a88ffb499b341c2eb
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Sat Nov 17 09:28:08 2018 -0800

    Lock xclbin prior to using KDS
    
    Fixes problem related to xclbin locking and icap reset of kds as part of AXI reset.  The AXI reset is performed when a process tries to download an xclbin (icap_download_bitstream_axlf) *and* that xclbin is unused (first download or already downloaded but unlocked).
    
    - P1 downloads xclbin calling xocl_read_axlf_helper
    -- not locked so resets AXI => resets KDS
    -- aquires xclbin lock (ref=1)
    -- releases xclbin lock (ref=0)
    - P1 configures scheduler
    -- This does not mess with xclbin locking, which remains ref=0
    -- Configure command enters KDS command queue
    -- P1 waits in execWait for configure command to complete
    - P2 downloads xclbin
    -- not locked so resets AXI => resets KDS
    -- The pending P1 configure command is ‘stale’ from KDSs perspective, this is the point of reset, so the command is removed
    -- acquires xclbin lock (ref=1)
    -- releases xclbin lock (ref=0)
    
    If P1 is slow getting serviced by KDS, P1 will never complete, it hangs in xclExecWait for configure command.
    
    The fix in this PR is to lock the xclbin for a client context prior to submitting a command to KDS.  The xclbin is locked only if necessary, no repeated attempts to lock an already locked xclbin.
    
    Error check that context locks the expected xclbin, not some xclbin swapped in by another process.

commit 9ce7921e162c77811df20ac15d5187b99dea0400
Author: hasansayani-xilinx <44008764+hasansayani-xilinx@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Fri Nov 9 15:37:42 2018 -0800

    XMA changes  (#642)
    
    * Fix issue wherein multiproc support was limited to same user id
    
    Signed-off-by: Jeffrey Mouroux <jmouroux@xilinx.com>
    
    * Fix issue wherein multiple device probes causes device programming to fail
    
    If two processes are started simultaneously, both will call our xma probe
    function at nearly the same time.  This will result in open device
    handles for both processes.  When one of these processes then attempts
    to program the device, it will fail.  This change serializes all
    access to the hardware from probe through to device programming to
    avoid this issue.  Once the device(s) is programmed, mutliple open
    device handles among multiple processes is no longer an issue.
    
    Signed-off-by: Jeffrey Mouroux <jmouroux@xilinx.com>
    
    * Initializing Plugin/Kernel allocations
    1. initializations
    2. checks in the tests
    (pending from libxmaapi : test case invocation)
    
    * Add PIDs to logs
    
    * Adding pic_order_cnt (POC) and pres_time_stamp (PTS) fields in XmaDataBuffers
        - requested by NGCodec
        - tested with Unit tests and building all apps/plugins
    
    Fixes #54

commit e4405de845b6cf304712b601bc638e08e6224227
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Sat Oct 27 19:49:17 2018 -0700

    Add CU stat accessed via sysfs for mb_scheduler subdevice (kds_custat)
    
    New control command ERT_CU_STAT collects  CU stat listing number of
    workgroups executed for each CU in an xclbin. The CU count is reset when ever a
    new xclbin is loaded.
    
    Supported both with and without embedded scheduler enabled.

    + Added hidden option to skip adding a validation image
    + Added ability to set the name of a section.
    + When an xclbin header is created, it is now initialized with the correct values (instead of all zeros).
    + When sections are added, the size of the section is now reported.
    + Refactor code to have only one constructure for a section.
    + Added DRCs to verify that only one section exists when adding sections via JSON
    + Add key-value pair support
    + Added support to add sections via a multiformatted JSON file.
    + Added multiplicty for the following options: --add-section, --remove-section, --dump-section, and --replace-section.

        Work Done
        * Fixed issue where the filelength for the xclbin wasn't being updated.  It is now.
          + Added support to update the xclbin's UUID when being written out.
          + Corrected issue where some TRACE statements were using string pointers as opposed to charater pointers.
        * Added support to replace a section in place via the option --replace-section.
        * Add buffer size validation to the MEM_TOPOLOGY, IP_LAYOUT, DEBUG_IP_LAYOUT, and CONNECTIVITY sections.  Buffers need to be less then 64K (which is what the drivers allocate space for).
        * Option modifications
        * Added verbosity option
        * Hid the trace and add-validation options
        * Added help after example messages when no options are given.
        * Added support when no options are given to produce some examples on how to use the command.
        * Updated XclBin::DumpSection() to support ParameterSectionData.
        * Updated XclBin::AddSection() to use the ParameterSectionData class
        * Created a regression test case for adding a section
        * xclbinutil is now build as one static image and the shared library is no longer used (but still is built)
        * Added --info option
        * Added section removal regression test
        * Change return type of XclBin::findSection to be const and made method public
        * Added const support
        * Added new class ParameterSectionData that will track the section, format, and filename for a given option.
        * Rename all of unittest exections from "cpp" to "cxx"
        * Added new FormatType enumeration values FT_UNDEFINED, FT_TXT, and FT_UNKNOWN.
        * Added new unit test UnitParameterSectinoData.cxx
        * Updated build to produce a shared and dynamic library for xclbinutil functionality.
        * Wrapped the static library usage with a xclbinutil.cxx executable wrapper
        * Updated the build to automatically pick up new unit tests
        * Created support to copy the new test_data directory to the build output enabling unit tests to work with their test data

commit 3f42175bbc587e853e33ebc1367dd441929e8cfc
Author: Gareth Edwards <gareth@xilinx.com>
Date:   Tue Sep 25 16:01:03 2018 +0100

    xrtdeps.sh - allow use of arbitrary sudo program
    
    Xilinx internal servers frequently use /tools/xgs/bin/sudo rather than
    a version of the tool on the normal system path. This change allows
    an environment variable called $SUDO to be used to point to the tool,
    otherwise if unset it reverts to the simple bare `sudo` command as
    before.

commit 3b2bfc25c2de9cae08fd489137f07c262f3df8a6
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Wed Sep 12 17:36:11 2018 -0700

    Update release version to 201802
    
    Versioning of packages and libraries reflect:
    
    Package version: <xilinx release>.<major>.<minor>.<patch>
    Library version: <major>.<minor>.<patch>
    SONAME encoded in runtime libraries: <major>.<minor>
    
    <major>: is bumped when incompatible changes goes into any runtime library
    <minor>: is bumped when new APIs are added to any runtime library
    <patch>: is bumped with every new build.  it should be reset when either <major> or <minor> is incremented.
    
    Example (2018.2_XDF):
    
    Package version: 201802.2.1.<patch>
    Library version: 2.1.<patch>
    SONAME: 2.1
    
    The patch level should follow the build number, except that with every
    <minor> or <major> increment, the patch number should restart.
    
    The SONAME in our runtime libraries will be encoded as
    <major>.<minor>, which implies that applications will have dynamic
    dependencies on this <major>.<minor> and won’t care about <patch>.

commit 5bb5391eae48abe3c44030d65b628104ec9b9bae
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Thu Aug 16 15:13:34 2018 -0700

    Do not throw bad_alloc if kernel argument bank check fails
    
    Kernel argument check is called during set_argument, but may not be
    able to do allocation check if the device context has multiple
    devices.  At the time the kernel argument is set the targeted device
    is unknown.  In other words, the argument cannot be allocated before
    an enqueue operation where the targeted device is known.

commit 7f011b2b9df490ff0eb3d2d67e402aa31711fc3d
Author: Lizhi Hou <36547078+houlz0507@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Aug 6 11:17:19 2018 -0700

    modified xbb device IDs (#174)
    
    Hi Lizhi, Hem,
    
    We made some slight updates to device IDs for the U* Boards. Please see the updated table here:
    
    http://confluence.xilinx.com/display/XSW/DSA+Tracker
    
    Note we’re reserved 4 PFs per board although today our DSAs only use 2. MGMT PF will be PF0 and User PF will be PF1 on these boards. Also for the MFG Device ID the driver should not pair when it sees this device ID because this is not a DSA and just the MFG Image which is used to recover the flash. Xbflash will have these special device IDs in its code so it recognizes the device IDs.

commit 750547c9d912207b7290613fd247e1925479e675
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Wed Aug 1 12:13:02 2018 -0700

    Fix xocl::memory synchronization when allocating boh
    
    There was a thread synchronization problem when BO was allocated
    as part of calling clSetKernelArg while an enqueue operation at the same
    time was trying allocate same BO.
    
    Additionally, a check for SW emulation was missing causing bank
    mismatch with host code.  Host code specified bank should be ignored
    in SW emu, where xclbin has no bank information.

commit 19fe47b2b47c1b72b8385fdb987c1ceff2e230cb
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Wed Aug 1 08:48:35 2018 -0700

    Fix ubuntu packaging when libraries are linked against version libraries
    
    The packager for DEBIAN does a dependency check on binaries.  If any
    dependent library cannot be found in library search path, then the
    dpkg-shlibdeps errors out.  This can be fixed in a couple of ways
    
    - Link libraries with RPATH set
    - Set LD_LIBRARY_PATH prior to invoking the dpkg-build
    - Change access mode on .so to executable
    - Disable SHLIB dependency check
    
    First is probably the better solution, but need more investigation.
    Second is not feasible since it is cmake that invokes the packager and
    we don't really know location it puts the libraries.  Thirds is just
    not good because .so should not be execuable.  Fourth is simplest and
    what was done in this commit.

    Fix sub-buffer offset bug

    shares the BO handle with the parent buffer.  When syncing a sub
    buffer, the offset of the sub buffer relative to the parent buffer was
    never considered, alas, syncing simply wrote/read from beginning of
    parent buffer.

commit d1d1857cc3be6ba2a6180bc539026716d5245b73
Merge: 0cac4b2 ec2bccc
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Mon Jul 23 11:40:43 2018 -0700

    Merge pull request #122 from stsoe/master
    
    Fix bug in device BO bank check in sw_emu

commit ec2bccc4e89f60e44f4ff3daaab77fef241e851a
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Mon Jul 23 10:22:44 2018 -0700

    Fix bug in device BO bank check in sw_emu
    Due to lacking memory topology in sw_emu, recent XRT changes (PR #28)
    incorrectly assumed that a memory buffer wasn't allocated on the
    device when in fact it was.
    
    A check to translate buffer device address into a device memory index
    failed because sw_emu doesn't have memory topology data to cross
    correlate buffer device address with corresponding bank.  Instead
    sw_emu must default such checks to some default memory index (0).

commit 4e48a96bd22f1f4d23f95bcf5b74e154dba248a5
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Wed Jun 27 16:21:11 2018 -0700

    Support memory bank buffer allocation without cl_ext pointer.
    
    This enhances current support without requiring single master
    connection for each CU.  A CU can now be connected to multiple memory
    banks, device buffer allocation happens as part of clSetKernelArg,
    where enough information is available to compute which bank to use.
    
    No changes required for exisitng code.
    
    To use the enhancemet, the host code should call clSetKernelArg
    immediately after clCreateBuffer and before clEnqueueMigrateMemObjects.
    This implies that a pipelined or ping-pong application should allocate
    a working set of buffers and kernel objects upfront and reuse these
    objects in the loop body withput calling clCreateKernel and
    clSetKernelArg in the body of the loop.

commit 1d68392efb1aead246b3f2207a99697566b6154e
Author: Soren Soe <soren.soe@xilinx.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 11 15:57:50 2018 -0700

    Pick up xrt library from install
    
    Introduced XILINX_XRT to override XILINX_SDX when looking for HAL
    level xrt library.  If XILINX_XRT is defined, then XILINX_SDX will not
    be searched.  If XILINX_XRT is not defined, then runtime will work as
    current 2018.2.  This is subject to change shortly once everyting is
    up and running.
